   vyatirekavākyamāha | tathā ca viparītavyatireko 'pi vakturaparādhād duṣṭaḥ	vyatireka vAkyam Aha | taTA ca viparIta vyatirekaH api vaktuH aparADAt duzwaH
   dṛṣṭāntadoṣānudāhṛtya duṣṭatvanibandhanatvaṃ darśayitumāha  na hayebhiriti	dRzwAnta dozAn udAhRtya duzwa tva nibanDana tvam darSayitum Aha na hayeBiH iti
   | sādhyaniyatapradarśanāya hi dṛṣṭāntā vaktavyāḥ | ebhiśca hetoḥ sapakṣa	| sADya niyata pradarSanAya hi dRzwAntAH vaktavyAH | eBiH ca hetoH sa pakza
   eva sattvaṃ vipakṣe ca sarvatrāsattvameva yat sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ tat	eva sattvam vipakze ca sarvatra asattvam eva yat sAmAnya lakzaNam tat 
   niścayena na śakyaṃ darśayitum |	niScayena na Sakyam darSayitum |
   nanu ca sāmānyalakṣaṇaṃ viśeṣaniyatameva pratipattavyam, na svata eva?	nanu ca sAmAnya lakzaNam viSeza niyatam eva pratipattavyam, na svatas eva?
   ityāha  viśeṣalakṣaṇaṃ vā | yadi viśeṣalakṣaṇaṃ pratipādayituṃ śakyeta,	iti Aha viSeza lakzaNam vA | yadi viSeza lakzaNam pratipAdayitum Sakyeta,
   syādeva sāmānyalakṣaṇapratipattiḥ | viśeṣalakṣaṇameva tu na śakyamebhiḥ	syAt eva sAmAnya lakzaNa pratipattiH | viSeza lakzaNam eva tu na Sakyam eBiH
   pratipādayitum | tasmādarthāpattyā sāmarthyena eṣāṃ nirākaraṇaṃ draṣṭavyam	pratipAdayitum | tasmAt arTa ApattyA sAmarTyena ezAm nirAkaraNam drazwavyam
   | sādhyaniyatasādhanapratītaye upātāḥ | tadasamarthā duṣṭāḥ,	| sADya niyata sADana pratItaye upAtAH | tat asamarTAH duzwAH,
   svakāryākaraṇāditi asāmarthyam || 136 ||	sva kArya akaraNAt iti asAmarTyam || 136 ||
   iyatā sāhanamuktam ||	iyatA sAhanam uktam ||
   dūṣaṇaṃ vaktumāha  duṣaṇeti | dūṣaṇā kā draṣṭavyā? nyūnatādonāmuktiḥ |	dUzaNam vaktum Aha duzaNa iti | dUzaNA kA drazwavyA? nyUna tA donAmuktiH |
   ucyate 'nayetyuktiḥ= vacanam | nyūnatādervacanam || 137 ||	ucyate anayeti uktiH vacanam | nyUna tA AdeH vacanam || 137 ||
   138 ye pūrva nyūnatādayaḥ sādhanadoṣā uktāsteṣāmudbhāvanaṃ dūṣaṇam tena	138 ye pUrva nyUna tA AdayaH sADana dozAH uktAH tezAm udBAvanam dUzaNam tena
   pareṣṭārthasiddhipratibandhāt ||	parezwa arTa sidDi pratibanDAt ||
   139 dūṣaṇābhāsāstu jātayaḥ |	139 dUzaNa ABAsAH tu jAtayaH |
   140 abhūtadoṣodbhāvanāni jātyuttarāṇīti ||	140 aBUta doza udBAvanAni jAti uttarANi iti ||
   tacca kasmāditi cet? tatrāha  teneti |	tat ca kasmAt iti cet? tatra aha tena iti |
   yasmāttena vacanena pūrvapakṣiṇā sādhayitumiṣṭasyārthasya siddhiḥ	yasmAt tena vacanena pUrva pakziNA sADayitum izwasya arTasya sidDiH
   pratibadhyate, tasmāt tad dūṣaṇam | tadetāni anudbhūtadūṣaṇāti || 138 ||	pratibaDyate, tasmAt tat dUzaNam | tat etAni anudBUta dUzaNAti || 138 ||
   jātaya eva dūṣaṇābhāsā viditavyāḥ || 139 ||	jAtayaH eva dUzaNa ABAsAH viditavyAH || 139 ||
   kāśca punastā jātaya iti? āha  abhūteti |	kAH ca punar tAH jAtayaH iti? Aha aBUta iti |
   na bhūto 'bhūtaḥ, abhūtā doṣā abhūtadoṣāḥ teṣāmudbhavanāni	na BUtaH aBUtaH, aBUtAH dozAH aBUta dozAH tezAm udBavanAni
   abhūtadoṣodbhāvanāni | yaiśca vacanaiḥ sādhanadoṣā abidhyamānā api	aBUta doza udBAvanAni | yEH ca vacanEH sADana dozAH abiDyamAnAH api
   udbhāvyante tāni jātayo veditavyāḥ |	udBAvyante tAni jAtayaH veditavyAH |
   samyagjñānanirūpaṇāvasare kathaṃ dūṣaṇa  tadābhāsānāmupadarśanamiti cet?	samyak jQAna nirUpaNa avasare kaTam dUzaNa tad ABAsAnAm upadarSanam iti ced ?
   ucyate, dūṣaṇānāṃ tayā dūṣaṇābhāsānāṃ ca nirūpaṇe samyagjñānamapi	ucyate, dUzaNAnAm tayA dUzaNa ABAsAnAm ca nirUpaNe samyak jQAnam api
   sasahāyaṃ nirūpitaṃ bhavatoti | tathā caitā hyatra dūṣaṇā iti tāsāṃ	sa sahAyam nirUpitam Bavatoti | taTA ca etAH hi atra dUzaNAH iti tAsAm
   pariharo vidheyaḥ | yadā vā ete dūṣaṇābhāsāḥ, etebhyaḥ śaṅkābhāva eva	pariharaH viDeyaH | yadA vE ete dUzaNa ABAsAH, eteByaH SaFkA BAvaH eva
   veditavya ityabhidhīyate, tadā samyagjñānameva sarvathā nirūpitaṃ bhavati	veditavyaH iti aBiDIyate, tadA samyak jQAnam eva sarvaTA nirUpitam Bavati
   | tasmād yathoktadoṣaprasaṅgo nāsti || 140 ||	| tasmAt yaTA ukta doza prasaFgaH na asti || 140 ||
   dūṣaṇaṃ vivarītumāha  ye pūrva nyūnatādayo 'siddhaviruddhānaikāntikā	dUzaNam vivarItum Aha ye pUrva nyUna tA AdayaH asidDa virudDa anEkAntikA
   uktāḥ, teṣāmudbhāvakaṃ yad vacanaṃ tad dūṣaṇam |	uktAH, tezAm udBAvakam yat vacanam tat dUzaNam |
   nanu ca nyūnatādayo na viparyayasādhanāḥ, tat kathaṃ dūṣaṇam? ityāha  tena	nanu ca nyUna tA AdayaH na viparyaya sADanAH, tat kaTam dUzaNam? iti Aha tena
   nyūnatādivacanena pareṣāmiṣṭaścāsāvarthaśca tasya siddhiḥ niścayaḥ, tasyāḥ	nyUna tA Adi vacanena pareza Am izwaH ca asO= arTaH ca tasya sidDiH niScayaH, tasyAH
   pratibandhāt | nāvaśyaṃ viparyayasādhanādeva dūṣaṇaṃ viruddhavat, api tu	pratibanDAt | na avaSyam viparyaya sADanAt eva dUzaNam virudDavat, api tu
   parasyābhipretaniścayavibandhānniścayābhāvo bhavati niścayaviparyaya	parasya aBipreta niScaya vibanDAt niScaya aBAvaH Bavati niScaya viparyaya
   ityastyeva viparyayasiddhiriti || 138 ||	iti asti eva viparyaya sidDiH iti || 138 ||
   uktā dūṣaṇā ||	uktA dUzaNAH ||
   dūṣaṇābhāsā iti | dūṣaṇavadābhāsanta iti dūṣaṇābhāṣā | ke te? jātaya iti |	dUzaNa ABAsAH iti | dUzaNa vat ABAsantaH iti dUzaNa ABAzA | ke te? jAtayaH iti |
   jātiśabdaḥ sādṛśyavacanaḥ | uttarasadṛśāni jātyuttarāṇi |	jAti SabdaH sAdRSya vacanaH | uttara sadRSAni jAti uttarANi |
   uttarasyāprayuktatvād uttarasadṛśāni jātyuttarāṇi || 139 ||	uttarasya aprayukta tvAt uttara sadRSAni jAti uttarANi || 139 ||
   tadevottarasādṛśyamuttarasthānaprayuktatvena darśayitumāha  abhūteti |	tat eva uttara sAdRSyam uttara sTAna prayukta tvena darSayitum Aha aBUta iti |
   abhūtasya asatyasya doṣasya udbhavanāni | udbhāvyata etairityaudbhāvanāni	aBUtasya asatyasya dozasya udBavanAni | udBAvyate etEH iti OdBAvanAni
   = vacanāni | tāni jātyuttarāṇi | jātyā sādṛśyenottarāṇi jātyuttarāṇīti ||	 vacanAni | tAni jAti uttarANi | jAtyA sAdRSyena uttarANi jAti uttarANi iti ||
   pṛthu yaccājitaṃ puṇyaṃ nyāyabidoḥ padaṃ padam |	pRTu yat ca ajitam puNyam nyAya bidoH padam padam |
   vyākhyānena mayādyaiva tato labdhvāmṛtaṃ dhruvam ||	vyAKyAnena mayA adya eva tatas labDvA amRtam Druvam ||
   prāṇikulamaśeṣaṃ hi yātu bhavaparikṣayam |	prANi kulam aSezam hi yAtu Bava parikzayam |
   yathocittena mārgeṇa nirdeśena nṛpasya ca ||	yaTocittena mArgeNa nirdeSena nRpasya ca ||
   iyaṃ vinītadevena śiṣyakalyāṇasiddhaye |	iyam vinIta devena Sizya kalyANa sidDaye |
   vistaro nāma ṭīkā hi nyāyabindorvinirmittā ||	vistaraH nAma wIkA hi nyAya bindoH vinirmittAH ||
   nyāyabinduvistaraṭīkāyāṃ śiṣyahitāyāṃ tṛtīyaḥ paricchedaḥ samāptaḥ ||	nyAya bindu vistarawIkAyAm Sizya hitAyAm tRtIyaH paricCedaH samAptaH ||
   sahastramekaṃ ślokānāṃ triśacślokāstathaiva ca |	sa hastram ekam SlokAnAm triSat SlokAH taTA eva ca |
   granthe vistaraṭīkāyāminoktaṃ paripiṇḍitam |	granTe vistarawI kAyAminA uktam paripiNxitam |
   ācāryavinītadevakṛtirnyāyabinduvistaraṭīkā śiṣyahitā samāptā ||	AcArya vinIta deva kRtiH nyAya binduvistarawIkA Sizya hitA samAptAH ||
   dharmottaraṭīkā	Darma uttarawIkA
   katipayapadavastuvyākhyayā yanmayāptam,	katipaya pada vastu vyAKyayA yat mayA Aptam,
   kuśalamamalamindoraṃśuvan nyāyabindoḥ ||	kuSalam amalam indoH aMSu vat nyAya bindoH ||
   padamajaramavāpya jñānadharmottaraṃ yad,	padam ajaram avApya jQAna Darma uttaram yat ,
   jagadūpakṛtimātravyāpṛtiḥ syāmato 'ham ||	jagadu upa kRti mAtra vyApRtiH syAm ataH aham ||
   ācāryadharmottaraviracittāyāṃ nyāyabinduṭīkāyāṃ tṛtīyaḥ pariccedaḥ	AcArya Darma uttara viracittAyAm nyAya binduwIkAyAm tRtIyaH pariccedaH
   samāptaḥ ||	samAptaH ||
   samāptaṃ ca nyāyabinduprakaraṇam ||	samAptam ca nyAya bindu prakaraNam ||
   ye dharmā hetuprabhavā hetuṃ teṣāṃ tathāgato hayavadat |	ye DarmAH hetu praBavAH hetum tezAm taTAgataH hayavadat |
   teṣāṃ ca yo nirodha evaṃvādī mahāśramaṇaḥ ||	tezAm ca yaH niroDaH evaMvAdI mahA ASramaNaH ||
